				openx.onload = function () { oxDone(); };
				node.parentNode.insertBefore(openx, node);
			})();

                    {minWidth: 641, value: 'tablet'},

  <script type="text/javascript">
   if (window.BEJSSDKObserver === undefined) {
  (function(BEJSSDKObserver, $, undefined) {
    var observer = void 0;
    var listeners = [];
    var readySet = [];
    var doc = window.document;
    var MutationObserver = window.MutationObserver || window.WebKitMutationObserver;

    function checkSelector(selector, fn, indexList) {
      var elements = doc.querySelectorAll(selector);
  /**
    issues on IE @see https://www.codesd.com/item/javascript-es6-not-a-function-error.html
    elements = Array.from(elements);

    */
    for (var i = 0, len = elements.length; i < len; i++) {
      /* -1 means all instances */
      if (indexList != -1 && !(i in indexList)) {
        continue;
      }
      var element = elements[i];
      for (var j = 0; j < readySet.length; j++) {
        if (readySet[j] == element.className || readySet[j] == element.id) {
          return;
        }
      }
      if (element.className) {
        readySet.push(element.className);
      }
      if (element.id) {
        readySet.push(element.id);
      }

      if (!element.ready || MutationObserver==null) {
        element.ready = true;
        fn.call(element, element);
      }
    }
  }

  function checkListeners() {
    listeners.forEach(function (listener) {
      return checkSelector(listener.selector, listener.fn, listener.indexList);
    });
  }

  function removeListener(selector, fn) {
    var i = listeners.length;
    while (i--) {
      var listener = listeners[i];
      if (listener.selector === selector && listener.fn === fn) {
        listeners.splice(i, 1);
        if (!listeners.length && observer) {
          observer.disconnect();
          observer = null;
        }
      }
    }
  }

/**
 * Fire event on first js selector
 * @param selector string to watch on
 * @param fn       callback function
 * @param index_list can be undefined which means only first one
 *                   or -1 which means all
 *                   or a list of allowable indexes
 */
 BEJSSDKObserver.jsElementReady = function(selector, fn, index_list) {
  if (index_list === undefined) {
    index_list = [];
    index_list.push(0);
  }

  if (MutationObserver != null) {
    if (!observer) {
      observer = new MutationObserver(checkListeners);
      observer.observe(doc.documentElement, {
        childList: true,
        subtree: true
      });
    }
    listeners.push({ selector: selector, fn: fn, indexList: index_list });
  } else {
    /* <= IE8 */
    if (!document.addEventListener) {
      /* log("<=IE8 attachEvent assignment"); */
      document.addEventListener = document.attachEvent;
    }
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(event) {
      var elements = doc.querySelectorAll(selector);
      for (var i = 0, len = elements.length; i < len; i++) {
        /* -1 means all instances */
        if (index_list != -1 && !(i in index_list)) {
          continue;
        }
        var element = elements[i];
        element.ready = true;
        fn.call(element, element);
      }
    });
  }

  checkSelector(selector, fn, index_list);
  return function () {
    return removeListener(selector, fn);
  };
};
}(window.BEJSSDKObserver = window.BEJSSDKObserver || {}));
}
var jsElementReady = window.BEJSSDKObserver.jsElementReady;

if (window.BELinkBlockGenerator === undefined) {
  (function(BELinkBlockGenerator, $, undefined) {
    BELinkBlockGenerator.MAXIMUM_HEADLINE_LENGTH = 100;
    BELinkBlockGenerator.MAXIMUM_DESC_LENGTH = 200;

    BELinkBlockGenerator.IND_LINK_BLOCK_TYPE_URL_TYPE = 0;
    BELinkBlockGenerator.IND_LINK_BLOCK_TYPE_HEADLINE_TYPE = 1;
    BELinkBlockGenerator.IND_LINK_BLOCK_TYPE_DESCRIPTION_TYPE = 2;
    BELinkBlockGenerator.IND_LINK_BLOCK_TYPE_IMAGE_TYPE = 3;

    BELinkBlockGenerator.REPLACEMENT_STRATEGY_OVERWRITE = 0;
    BELinkBlockGenerator.REPLACEMENT_STRATEGY_POST_APPEND_ELEMENT = 1;
    BELinkBlockGenerator.REPLACEMENT_STRATEGY_PRE_APPEND_ELEMENT = 2;
    BELinkBlockGenerator.REPLACEMENT_STRATEGY_PRE_APPEND_PARENT = 3;

    BELinkBlockGenerator.setMaximumHeadlineLength = function(length) {
      BELinkBlockGenerator.MAXIMUM_HEADLINE_LENGTH = length;
    };

    BELinkBlockGenerator.setMaximumDescriptionLength = function(length) {
      BELinkBlockGenerator.MAXIMUM_DESC_LENGTH = length;
    };

    BELinkBlockGenerator.generateIndividualLinks = function(parentElement, linkStructure, link) {
      var link_level_element_tag = linkStructure[0];
      var link_level_element = document.createElement(link_level_element_tag);
      var link_attribute_dictionary = linkStructure[1];
      var allowable_elements = linkStructure[2];
      var children_link_structures = linkStructure[3];
      for (var link_attribute_key in link_attribute_dictionary) {
        link_level_element.setAttribute(link_attribute_key, link_attribute_dictionary[link_attribute_key]);
      }

      var added_something = false;
      if (allowable_elements.indexOf(BELinkBlockGenerator.IND_LINK_BLOCK_TYPE_URL_TYPE)>=0) {
        link_level_element.setAttribute('href', link.url);
        added_something = true;
      }
      if (allowable_elements.indexOf(BELinkBlockGenerator.IND_LINK_BLOCK_TYPE_HEADLINE_TYPE)>=0 && link.h1) {
        var headline_text = link.h1;
        if (headline_text.length > BELinkBlockGenerator.MAXIMUM_HEADLINE_LENGTH) {
          headline_text = headline_text.substring(0, BELinkBlockGenerator.MAXIMUM_HEADLINE_LENGTH) + '...';
        }
        var text_node = document.createTextNode(headline_text);
        link_level_element.appendChild(text_node);
        added_something = true;
      }
      if (allowable_elements.indexOf(BELinkBlockGenerator.IND_LINK_BLOCK_TYPE_DESCRIPTION_TYPE)>=0 && link.desc) {
        var desc_text = link.desc;
        if (desc_text.length > BELinkBlockGenerator.MAXIMUM_DESC_LENGTH) {
          desc_text = desc_text.substring(0, BELinkBlockGenerator.MAXIMUM_DESC_LENGTH) + '...';
        }
        var text_node = document.createTextNode(desc_text);
        link_level_element.appendChild(text_node);
        added_something = true;
      }
      if (allowable_elements.indexOf(BELinkBlockGenerator.IND_LINK_BLOCK_TYPE_IMAGE_TYPE)>=0 && link.image) {
        link_level_element.setAttribute('src', link.image);
        added_something = true;
      }
/**
    don't emit for empty links, desc, headline, image
    except for parent structures where allowable_length=0
    */
    if (!added_something && allowable_elements.length != 0) {

      return;
    }
    /* go depth first */
    for (var childrenIndex=0; childrenIndex<children_link_structures.length; childrenIndex++) {
      var childLinkStructure = children_link_structures[childrenIndex];
      BELinkBlockGenerator.generateIndividualLinks(link_level_element, childLinkStructure, link);
    }
    parentElement.appendChild(link_level_element);
  };

  BELinkBlockGenerator.insertLinkBlocks = function(targetElement, replacementStrategy, overallStructure, linkStructure, links,
                                                   titleStructure) {
    if (targetElement == null) {
      return;
    }

    if (replacementStrategy == BELinkBlockGenerator.REPLACEMENT_STRATEGY_OVERWRITE) {
      while (targetElement.firstChild) {
        targetElement.removeChild(targetElement.firstChild);
      }
    }

    var previousElement = targetElement;
    for (var i=0;i<overallStructure.length;i++) {
      var level_definition = overallStructure[i];
      var level_element_tag = level_definition[0];
      var level_element = document.createElement(level_element_tag);
      var attribute_dictionary = level_definition[1];
      for (var attribute_key in attribute_dictionary) {
        level_element.setAttribute(attribute_key, attribute_dictionary[attribute_key]);
      }

      /* need to place title structure */
      if (titleStructure && titleStructure[0] == i) {
        var title_element_tag = titleStructure[1];
        var title_element = document.createElement(title_element_tag);
        var title_attribute_dictionary = titleStructure[2];
        var title_text_content = titleStructure[3];
        for (var title_attribute_key in title_attribute_dictionary) {
          title_element.setAttribute(title_attribute_key, title_attribute_dictionary[title_attribute_key]);
        }

        var title_text_node = document.createTextNode(title_text_content);
        title_element.appendChild(title_text_node);


        level_element.appendChild(title_element);
      }

      /* last level place links */
      if (i == overallStructure.length-1) {
        for (var link_i=0; link_i < links.length; link_i++) {
          var link = links[link_i];
          for (var linkStructureIndex=0;linkStructureIndex < linkStructure.length; linkStructureIndex++) {
            BELinkBlockGenerator.generateIndividualLinks(level_element, linkStructure[linkStructureIndex], link)
          }
        }
      }

      /* first level child we need to check placement */
      if (previousElement == targetElement) {
        if (replacementStrategy == BELinkBlockGenerator.REPLACEMENT_STRATEGY_PRE_APPEND_ELEMENT) {
          /* 2 means insert right before */
          previousElement.insertBefore(level_element, targetElement.firstChild);
        } else if (replacementStrategy == BELinkBlockGenerator.REPLACEMENT_STRATEGY_PRE_APPEND_PARENT) {
          /* 3 means insert right before at parent level */
          var parentElement = previousElement.parentElement;
          parentElement.insertBefore(level_element, previousElement);
        } else {
          previousElement.appendChild(level_element);
        }
      } else {
        previousElement.appendChild(level_element);
      }
      previousElement = level_element;
    }
  };
}(window.BELinkBlockGenerator = window.BELinkBlockGenerator || {}))
};
  </script>

      <div class="tabs-with-image__main">
       <div class="section-title">
        <h2 class="section-title__text">
         AKC Cares
        </h2>
       </div>
       <div class="tabs tabs--active-border tabs--dark" data-accordion-content=".tabs__tab-panel-content" data-accordion-panel=".tabs__tab-panel" data-accordion-trigger=".tabs__panel-trigger" data-js-component="accordionToTabs" data-panels=".tabs__tab-panel" data-tabs=".tabs__tabs">
        <div class="show-at-medium">
         <ul class="tabs__tabs">
          <li class="tabs__single-tab">
           <a class="tabs__anchor" href="javascript:void(0);" id="anchor-AKC Canine Health Foundation">

             <div>
              AKC Canine Health Foundation
             </div>
            </div>
           </a>
          </li>
          <li class="tabs__single-tab">
           <a class="tabs__anchor" href="javascript:void(0);" id="anchor-Rescue Network">
            <div class="tabs__inner-content">
             <div>

          </li>
          <li class="tabs__single-tab">
           <a class="tabs__anchor" href="javascript:void(0);" id="anchor-AKC Reunite">

          <li class="tabs__single-tab">

           </a>
          </li>
          <li class="tabs__single-tab">
           <a class="tabs__anchor" href="javascript:void(0);" id="anchor-Museum of the Dog">

             </div>
            </div>
           </a>
          </li>
          <li class="tabs__single-tab">
           <a class="tabs__anchor" href="javascript:void(0);" id="anchor-Protecting Your Rights">
            <div class="tabs__inner-content">
             <div>
              Protecting Your Rights
             </div>
            </div>
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
        </div>
        <div class="tabs__panel-wrap">
         <div class="tabs__tab-panel" data-panel-index="0" id="panel-AKC Canine Health Foundation">
          <div class="tabs__tab-panel-content">
           <div class="hide-at-medium">
            <div class="tabs__mobile-header">
             <h2 class="tabs__panel-title">
              AKC Canine Health Foundation
             </h2>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="show-at-medium">
            <h2 class="tabs__panel-title">
             AKC Canine Health Foundation
            </h2>
           </div>
           <p>
            The AKC Canine Health Foundation is a nonprofit organization dedicated to the prevention and treatment of diseases in all dogs. Since 1995, we’ve been awarding grants to scientists and professionals to advance canine health research, while providing professional information and resources for today’s dog owner.
           </p>
           <a class="button button--ghost button--ghost-transparent" href="http://www.akcchf.org" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Learn More
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="tabs__tab-panel" data-panel-index="1" id="panel-Rescue Network">
          <div class="tabs__tab-panel-content">
           <div class="hide-at-medium">
            <div class="tabs__mobile-header">
             <h2 class="tabs__panel-title">
              Rescue Network
             </h2>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="show-at-medium">
            <h2 class="tabs__panel-title">
             Rescue Network
            </h2>
           </div>
           <p>
            The AKC Rescue Network is the largest network of dog rescue groups in the U.S., with more than 450 groups providing fostering and rehabilitation services.
           </p>
           <a class="button button--ghost button--ghost-transparent" href="https://www.akc.org/dog-breeds/rescue-network/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Learn More
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="tabs__tab-panel" data-panel-index="2" id="panel-AKC Reunite">
          <div class="tabs__tab-panel-content">
           <div class="hide-at-medium">
            <div class="tabs__mobile-header">
             <h2 class="tabs__panel-title">
              AKC Reunite
             </h2>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="show-at-medium">
            <h2 class="tabs__panel-title">
             AKC Reunite
            </h2>
           </div>
           <p>
            AKC Reunite is North America’s largest not for profit pet ID and recovery service, providing microchipping and ID services as well as a national recovery database to safely return dogs home should they get lost and, through AKC Pet Disaster Relief, helping local Emergency Management to provide animal care services immediately following disasters.
           </p>
           <a class="button button--ghost button--ghost-transparent" href="http://www.akcreunite.org/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Learn More
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="tabs__tab-panel" data-panel-index="3" id="panel-Humane Fund">
          <div class="tabs__tab-panel-content">
           <div class="hide-at-medium">
            <div class="tabs__mobile-header">
             <h2 class="tabs__panel-title">
              Humane Fund
             </h2>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="show-at-medium">
            <h2 class="tabs__panel-title">
             Humane Fund
            </h2>
           </div>
           <p>
            The AKC Humane Fund offers grants and resources to pet-related organizations across the nation for educating the public about responsible dog ownership.
           </p>
           <a class="button button--ghost button--ghost-transparent" href="https://www.akchumanefund.org/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Learn More
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="tabs__tab-panel" data-panel-index="4" id="panel-Museum of the Dog">
          <div class="tabs__tab-panel-content">
           <div class="hide-at-medium">
            <div class="tabs__mobile-header">
             <h2 class="tabs__panel-title">
              Museum of the Dog
             </h2>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="show-at-medium">
            <h2 class="tabs__panel-title">
             Museum of the Dog
            </h2>
           </div>
           <p>
            The AKC Museum of the Dog is dedicated to the collection, preservation, exhibition, and interpretation of the art, artifacts and literature of the dog for the purposes of education, historical perspective, aesthetic enjoyment and in order to enhance the appreciation for and knowledge of the significance of the dog and the human/canine relationship.
           </p>
           <a class="button button--ghost button--ghost-transparent" href="https://museumofthedog.org/">
            Learn More
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="tabs__tab-panel" data-panel-index="5" id="panel-Protecting Your Rights">
          <div class="tabs__tab-panel-content">
           <div class="hide-at-medium">
            <div class="tabs__mobile-header">
             <h2 class="tabs__panel-title">
              Protecting Your Rights
             </h2>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="show-at-medium">
            <h2 class="tabs__panel-title">
             Protecting Your Rights
            </h2>
           </div>
           <p>
            The Government Relations Department (GR) leads advocacy and legislative efforts to protect the rights of all dog owners, promote responsible dog ownership and ensure that laws governing dog ownership and breeding are reasonable, enforceable and non-discriminatory. AKC GR monitors and addresses canine legislation that impacts dog ownership, and is pleased to offer a wide range of educational materials, policy resources and assistance to dog owners, club/community leaders and policymakers alike.
           </p>
           <a class="button button--ghost button--ghost-transparent" href="http://akc.org/clubs-delegates/government-relations/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Learn More
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="tabs-with-image__aside show-at-medium">
       <img alt="Beagle playing with his owner at home." class="attachment-large_portrait size-large_portrait lozad" data-sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" data-src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01150926/Beagle-playing-with-his-owner-at-home.jpg" data-srcset="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01150926/Beagle-playing-with-his-owner-at-home.jpg 500w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01150926/Beagle-playing-with-his-owner-at-home-200x300.jpg 200w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01150926/Beagle-playing-with-his-owner-at-home-341x512.jpg 341w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01150926/Beagle-playing-with-his-owner-at-home-424x636.jpg 424w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01150926/Beagle-playing-with-his-owner-at-home-33x50.jpg 33w" height="750" src="https://www.akc.org/wp-content/themes/akc/component-library/assets/img/1x1.trans.gif" width="500"/>
      </div>
     </div>
    </div>
   </div>
   <section class="page-section page-home__events-slider">
    <div class="event-slider event-slider--none-spacing event-slider--none-borders" data-js-component="eventSlider">
     <div class="event-slider__header pb7">
      <div class="section-title section-title--center">
       <h2 class="section-title__text">
        Sports &amp; Events
       </h2>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="event-slider__wrap">
      <div class="event-slider__inner page-container">
       <div class="event-slider__slide">
        <a class="event" href="http://akc.org/sports/conformation/">
         <img alt="Golden Retriever at the AKC National Championship." class="event__image lozad" data-sizes="(max-width: 280px) 100vw, 280px" data-src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/02160918/Golden-Retriever-at-the-AKC-National-Championship.jpg" data-srcset="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/02160918/Golden-Retriever-at-the-AKC-National-Championship.jpg 280w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/02160918/Golden-Retriever-at-the-AKC-National-Championship-150x150.jpg 150w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/02160918/Golden-Retriever-at-the-AKC-National-Championship-50x50.jpg 50w" height="280" src="https://www.akc.org/wp-content/themes/akc/component-library/assets/img/1x1.trans.gif" width="280"/>
         <div class="event__title-area mt4 mb2">
          <h3 class="event__title my0">
           Conformation
          </h3>
         </div>
         <div class="event__body">
          Dog shows (officially conformation) may look like beauty pageants, but they’re not. Dogs aren’t compared against each other; they’re compared against the standards of their breed.
         </div>
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="event-slider__slide">
        <a class="event" href="http://akc.org/sports/agility/">
         <img alt="Flat Coated Retriever leaping over an agility jump." class="event__image lozad" data-sizes="(max-width: 280px) 100vw, 280px" data-src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01153552/Flat-Coated-Retriever-leaping-over-an-agility-jump.jpg" data-srcset="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01153552/Flat-Coated-Retriever-leaping-over-an-agility-jump.jpg 280w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01153552/Flat-Coated-Retriever-leaping-over-an-agility-jump-150x150.jpg 150w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01153552/Flat-Coated-Retriever-leaping-over-an-agility-jump-50x50.jpg 50w" height="280" src="https://www.akc.org/wp-content/themes/akc/component-library/assets/img/1x1.trans.gif" width="280"/>
         <div class="event__title-area mt4 mb2">
          <h3 class="event__title my0">
           Agility
          </h3>
         </div>
         <div class="event__body">
          An exhilarating way to exercise with your dog, Agility is a fast-paced obstacle course with tunnels, hurdles, and other challenges that your dog completes as quickly as possible.
         </div>
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="event-slider__slide">
        <a class="event" href="http://akc.org/sports/rally/">
         <img alt="Labrador Retriever in a Junior Rally trail." class="event__image lozad" data-sizes="(max-width: 400px) 100vw, 400px" data-src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/10/13002621/Rally-hero-3-400x400.jpg" data-srcset="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/10/13002621/Rally-hero-3-400x400.jpg 400w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/10/13002621/Rally-hero-3-150x150.jpg 150w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/10/13002621/Rally-hero-3-500x500.jpg 500w" height="400" src="https://www.akc.org/wp-content/themes/akc/component-library/assets/img/1x1.trans.gif" width="400"/>
         <div class="event__title-area mt4 mb2">
          <h3 class="event__title my0">
           Rally
          </h3>
         </div>
         <div class="event__body">
          In Rally, you and your dog navigate a course, side-by-side, through 10-20 different exercises and, although it’s timed, it's more about proving excellent behavior and teamwork than speed.
         </div>
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="event-slider__slide">
        <a class="event" href="http://akc.org/sports/coursing/fast-cat/">
         <img alt="" class="event__image lozad" data-sizes="(max-width: 400px) 100vw, 400px" data-src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/10141328/fastest-dog-usa-frenchie-400x400.jpg" data-srcset="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/10141328/fastest-dog-usa-frenchie-400x400.jpg 400w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/10141328/fastest-dog-usa-frenchie-150x150.jpg 150w" height="400" src="https://www.akc.org/wp-content/themes/akc/component-library/assets/img/1x1.trans.gif" width="400"/>
         <div class="event__title-area mt4 mb2">
          <h3 class="event__title my0">
           Fast CAT
          </h3>
         </div>
         <div class="event__body">
          This fast-paced event features one dog running at a time, with their speed clocked and converted to MPH. Any dog over 12 months of age that are registered or enrolled with the AKC can participate.
         </div>
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="event-slider__slide">
        <a class="event" href="http://akc.org/sports/akc-scent-work/">
         <img alt="Bulldog in a scent work trial." class="event__image lozad" data-sizes="(max-width: 280px) 100vw, 280px" data-src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01161046/Bulldog-in-a-scent-work-trial.jpg" data-srcset="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01161046/Bulldog-in-a-scent-work-trial.jpg 280w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01161046/Bulldog-in-a-scent-work-trial-150x150.jpg 150w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01161046/Bulldog-in-a-scent-work-trial-50x50.jpg 50w" height="280" src="https://www.akc.org/wp-content/themes/akc/component-library/assets/img/1x1.trans.gif" width="280"/>
         <div class="event__title-area mt4 mb2">
          <h3 class="event__title my0">
           Scent Work
          </h3>
         </div>
         <div class="event__body">
          In AKC Scent Work, the handler guides the dog through a set search area to find specific odors that the dogs have been trained to detect.
         </div>
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="event-slider__slide">
        <a class="event" href="http://akc.org/sports/obedience/">
         <img alt="Golden Retrievers in an obedience trial." class="event__image lozad" data-sizes="(max-width: 280px) 100vw, 280px" data-src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/02160926/Golden-Retrievers-in-an-obedience-trial.jpg" data-srcset="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/02160926/Golden-Retrievers-in-an-obedience-trial.jpg 280w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/02160926/Golden-Retrievers-in-an-obedience-trial-150x150.jpg 150w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/02160926/Golden-Retrievers-in-an-obedience-trial-50x50.jpg 50w" height="280" src="https://www.akc.org/wp-content/themes/akc/component-library/assets/img/1x1.trans.gif" width="280"/>
         <div class="event__title-area mt4 mb2">
          <h3 class="event__title my0">
           Obedience
          </h3>
         </div>
         <div class="event__body">
          Developed in the 1930s, Obedience is one of our oldest sporting events and is open to all breeds. From walking in figure eights to sitting for 1-3 minutes, dogs show off their good behavior.
         </div>
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="event-slider__slide">
        <a class="event" href="http://akc.org/sports/tracking/">
         <img alt="Bloodhound on a scent in the woods." class="event__image lozad" data-sizes="(max-width: 280px) 100vw, 280px" data-src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/02160929/Bloodhound-on-a-scent-in-the-woods.jpg" data-srcset="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/02160929/Bloodhound-on-a-scent-in-the-woods.jpg 280w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/02160929/Bloodhound-on-a-scent-in-the-woods-150x150.jpg 150w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/02160929/Bloodhound-on-a-scent-in-the-woods-50x50.jpg 50w" height="280" src="https://www.akc.org/wp-content/themes/akc/component-library/assets/img/1x1.trans.gif" width="280"/>
         <div class="event__title-area mt4 mb2">
          <h3 class="event__title my0">
           Tracking
          </h3>
         </div>
         <div class="event__body">
          Your dog’s natural ability to recognize and follow a scent is on full display in AKC Tracking events.
         </div>
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="event-slider__slide">
        <a class="event" href="http://akc.org/sports/herding/">
         <img alt="Shetland Sheepdog herding sheep." class="event__image lozad" data-sizes="(max-width: 280px) 100vw, 280px" data-src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01154114/Shetland-Sheepdog-herding-sheep.jpg" data-srcset="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01154114/Shetland-Sheepdog-herding-sheep.jpg 280w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01154114/Shetland-Sheepdog-herding-sheep-150x150.jpg 150w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01154114/Shetland-Sheepdog-herding-sheep-50x50.jpg 50w" height="280" src="https://www.akc.org/wp-content/themes/akc/component-library/assets/img/1x1.trans.gif" width="280"/>
         <div class="event__title-area mt4 mb2">
          <h3 class="event__title my0">
           Herding
          </h3>
         </div>
         <div class="event__body">
          In the sport of Herding, your dog uses his innate herding abilities to move sheep (or other animals) around a field.
         </div>
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="event-slider__slide">
        <a class="event" href="http://akc.org/sports/earthdog/">
         <img alt="Scottish Terrier participating in an Earthdog trial." class="event__image lozad" data-sizes="(max-width: 400px) 100vw, 400px" data-src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/12221832/earthdog-400x400.jpg" data-srcset="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/12221832/earthdog-400x400.jpg 400w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/12221832/earthdog-150x150.jpg 150w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/12221832/earthdog-300x300.jpg 300w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/12221832/earthdog-511x512.jpg 511w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/12221832/earthdog-500x500.jpg 500w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/11/12221832/earthdog.jpg 617w" height="400" src="https://www.akc.org/wp-content/themes/akc/component-library/assets/img/1x1.trans.gif" width="400"/>
         <div class="event__title-area mt4 mb2">
          <h3 class="event__title my0">
           Earth Dog
          </h3>
         </div>
         <div class="event__body">
          Open to small terriers and Dachshunds, Earthdog tests are non-competitive and assess your dog’s abilities for seeking and locating prey underground.
         </div>
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="event-slider__slide">
        <a class="event" href="http://akc.org/sports/pointing-breeds/">
         <img alt="Pointer hunting in the fall." class="event__image lozad" data-sizes="(max-width: 280px) 100vw, 280px" data-src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01154618/Pointer-hunting-in-the-fall.jpg" data-srcset="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01154618/Pointer-hunting-in-the-fall.jpg 280w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01154618/Pointer-hunting-in-the-fall-150x150.jpg 150w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01154618/Pointer-hunting-in-the-fall-50x50.jpg 50w" height="280" src="https://www.akc.org/wp-content/themes/akc/component-library/assets/img/1x1.trans.gif" width="280"/>
         <div class="event__title-area mt4 mb2">
          <h3 class="event__title my0">
           Field Trials
          </h3>
         </div>
         <div class="event__body">
          Since 1924, these competitions give your pointing breed a chance to show how fast he can run and his keen desire to hunt for and find game.
         </div>
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="event-slider__slide">
        <a class="event" href="http://akc.org/sports/basset-hound-field-trials/hunting/">
         <img alt="Sussex Spaniel carrying game in a field." class="event__image lozad" data-sizes="(max-width: 280px) 100vw, 280px" data-src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01155139/Sussex-Spaniel-carrying-game-in-a-field.jpg" data-srcset="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01155139/Sussex-Spaniel-carrying-game-in-a-field.jpg 280w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01155139/Sussex-Spaniel-carrying-game-in-a-field-150x150.jpg 150w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01155139/Sussex-Spaniel-carrying-game-in-a-field-50x50.jpg 50w" height="280" src="https://www.akc.org/wp-content/themes/akc/component-library/assets/img/1x1.trans.gif" width="280"/>
         <div class="event__title-area mt4 mb2">
          <h3 class="event__title my0">
           Hunting
          </h3>
         </div>
         <div class="event__body">
          Hunting tests are designed to test a dog's ability to work with their human hunting companion in a simulated hunting situation.
         </div>
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="event-slider__slide">
        <a class="event" href="http://akc.org/sports/herding/farm-dog-certified-test/">
         <img alt="Norwegian Buhund laying atop a bale of hay." class="event__image lozad" data-sizes="(max-width: 280px) 100vw, 280px" data-src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/07151150/Norwegian-Buhund-laying-atop-a-bale-of-hay.jpg" data-srcset="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/07151150/Norwegian-Buhund-laying-atop-a-bale-of-hay.jpg 280w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/07151150/Norwegian-Buhund-laying-atop-a-bale-of-hay-150x150.jpg 150w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/07151150/Norwegian-Buhund-laying-atop-a-bale-of-hay-50x50.jpg 50w" height="280" src="https://www.akc.org/wp-content/themes/akc/component-library/assets/img/1x1.trans.gif" width="280"/>
         <div class="event__title-area mt4 mb2">
          <h3 class="event__title my0">
           Farm Dog Certified
          </h3>
         </div>
         <div class="event__body">
          The Farm Dog Certified test is a series of twelve exercises in a noncompetitive pass/fail evaluation and open to all dogs over nine months that are registered or enrolled with the AKC.
         </div>
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="event-slider__slide">
        <a class="event" href="http://akc.org/sports/coursing/lure-coursing/">
         <img alt="Italian Greyhound running wearing a lure coursing jersey." class="event__image lozad" data-sizes="(max-width: 280px) 100vw, 280px" data-src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01155859/Italian-Greyhound-running.jpg" data-srcset="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01155859/Italian-Greyhound-running.jpg 280w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01155859/Italian-Greyhound-running-150x150.jpg 150w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01155859/Italian-Greyhound-running-50x50.jpg 50w" height="280" src="https://www.akc.org/wp-content/themes/akc/component-library/assets/img/1x1.trans.gif" width="280"/>
         <div class="event__title-area mt4 mb2">
          <h3 class="event__title my0">
           Lure Coursing
          </h3>
         </div>
         <div class="event__body">
          The lure will lead a pack to run as fast as they can, zig-zagging across an open field in hopes of catching it. The test is a basic performance of coursing that is non-competitive and is pass/fail.
         </div>
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="event-slider__slide">
        <a class="event" href="http://akc.org/sports/coursing/coursing-ability-test/">
         <img alt="Chinese Shar Pei running in a coursing ability trial." class="event__image lozad" data-sizes="(max-width: 280px) 100vw, 280px" data-src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01155902/Chinese-Shar-Pei-running.jpg" data-srcset="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01155902/Chinese-Shar-Pei-running.jpg 280w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01155902/Chinese-Shar-Pei-running-150x150.jpg 150w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01155902/Chinese-Shar-Pei-running-50x50.jpg 50w" height="280" src="https://www.akc.org/wp-content/themes/akc/component-library/assets/img/1x1.trans.gif" width="280"/>
         <div class="event__title-area mt4 mb2">
          <h3 class="event__title my0">
           Coursing Ability
          </h3>
         </div>
         <div class="event__body">
          Most dogs have the urge to chase different objects, whether it's a ball or each other during playtime. CAT is a non-competitive, pass/fail event that harnesses their natural instinct.
         </div>
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="event-slider__slide">
        <a class="event" href="http://akc.org/sports/coonhound/">
         <img alt="Black and Tan Coonhound standing in the forest in the fall." class="event__image lozad" data-sizes="(max-width: 280px) 100vw, 280px" data-src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01160436/Black-and-Tan-Coonhound-standing-in-the-forest-in-the-fall.jpg" data-srcset="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01160436/Black-and-Tan-Coonhound-standing-in-the-forest-in-the-fall.jpg 280w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01160436/Black-and-Tan-Coonhound-standing-in-the-forest-in-the-fall-150x150.jpg 150w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01160436/Black-and-Tan-Coonhound-standing-in-the-forest-in-the-fall-50x50.jpg 50w" height="280" src="https://www.akc.org/wp-content/themes/akc/component-library/assets/img/1x1.trans.gif" width="280"/>
         <div class="event__title-area mt4 mb2">
          <h3 class="event__title my0">
           Coonhound
          </h3>
         </div>
         <div class="event__body">
          Nite Hunts require coonhounds to hunt at night with a handler and be scored on their ability to trail and tree a raccoon. It is fun to watch and the hounds enjoy doing what they were meant to do!
         </div>
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="event-slider__slide">
        <a class="event" href="http://akc.org/sports/trick-dog/about-trick-dog/">
         <img alt="German Pinscher in a Trick Dog demonstration." class="event__image lozad" data-sizes="(max-width: 280px) 100vw, 280px" data-src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01161447/Trick-Dog-demonstration.jpg" data-srcset="https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01161447/Trick-Dog-demonstration.jpg 280w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01161447/Trick-Dog-demonstration-150x150.jpg 150w, https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn-origin-etr.akc.org/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/01161447/Trick-Dog-demonstration-50x50.jpg 50w" height="280" src="https://www.akc.org/wp-content/themes/akc/component-library/assets/img/1x1.trans.gif" width="280"/>
         <div class="event__title-area mt4 mb2">
          <h3 class="event__title my0">
           Trick Dog
          </h3>
         </div>
         <div class="event__body">
          Since the 1920s and '40s when trick dogs such as Rin Tin Tin and Lassie won peoples’ hearts, trick dog training has become one of the most exciting new areas in dog training today.
         </div>
        </a>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="event-slider__nav-wrap">
       <div class="slider-dot-nav">
        <div class="slider-dot-nav__nav-area">

       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="side-by-side__content">
       <div class="side-by-side__content-wrap">
        <div class="content-block">
         <h2 class="content-block__title mb4">
          Register Your Dog
         </h2>
         <h3 class="content-block__subtitle mt0 mb3">
          Learn Why
         </h3>
         <div class="content-block__text">
          <p>
           Having a dog is a lifelong journey. Let the AKC be there to support you along the way. Complete your lifetime registration today and access AKC's Canine Care packages, which include essential resources and services available to you throughout every stage of your dog's life.
          </p>
         </div>
         <div class="content-block__bottom-content">
          <div class="content-block__button">
           <a class="button" href="http://akc.org/register/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Learn More
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
